###  Selänne₁

This rare proper noun overlaps more common *Selänne* (FIXME)
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  48
* Origin:  finer|enwikt
* Possible NER class:  GEO
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
